if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/_overview');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/_overview');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/_overview') != '63be1b103bd825b0e35ddfc74a137f7f277b57c7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/_overview', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/_overview');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== '63be1b103bd825b0e35ddfc74a137f7f277b57c7') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== 'b31f189912dac1ee04509cb8c75d2b047ac5b51b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/_overview');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/_overview');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/_overview')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/_overview', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== '63be1b103bd825b0e35ddfc74a137f7f277b57c7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '5a3a78a1acf4b8e4bb25279888a2d7fa202fddb8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5a3a78a1acf4b8e4bb25279888a2d7fa202fddb8') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '7a785fe482fe741c30c91b75c7803b46fae6b063') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5a3a78a1acf4b8e4bb25279888a2d7fa202fddb8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') != 'd74fa60ea1c3631384a615a28d4b1663b174df65') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'd74fa60ea1c3631384a615a28d4b1663b174df65') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'b3f8be54cff8a4e7f355fe84517a429b0193e566') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'd74fa60ea1c3631384a615a28d4b1663b174df65') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	writefile_16();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') != '51c3fb5b7ea03c6c61e43bfdc8ae31459498550e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '51c3fb5b7ea03c6c61e43bfdc8ae31459498550e') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '14ca1d0d53bf5d497e23c8716bf9b4e3931df819') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '51c3fb5b7ea03c6c61e43bfdc8ae31459498550e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php') != '9ef8e0f259e3497ef82cbcf3ff351439dad04e71') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php') !== '9ef8e0f259e3497ef82cbcf3ff351439dad04e71') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php') !== '22c1feaa8ad843963a89a5716e98083fe534fe87') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php') !== '9ef8e0f259e3497ef82cbcf3ff351439dad04e71') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusAuthUtils.class.php');

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_21();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '9966f2ed3c1c7a273974f9bdbb8dc0bfceb6fbdd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '9966f2ed3c1c7a273974f9bdbb8dc0bfceb6fbdd') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '74340406db74063a021fbb401411e618d62b00c7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_21();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '9966f2ed3c1c7a273974f9bdbb8dc0bfceb6fbdd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	writefile_24();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') != '16609e886e02c9c553c3c1d927d711a1c6379488') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '16609e886e02c9c553c3c1d927d711a1c6379488') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'ede0b69613ee18254ff03ee7216921432f265cad') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_24();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '16609e886e02c9c553c3c1d927d711a1c6379488') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_25();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != '59b114803469b1fe3f4068304b4032bd428dd2cc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '59b114803469b1fe3f4068304b4032bd428dd2cc') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'a347255137c8a18898ffd3b466a6e8f9bb7ff354') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '59b114803469b1fe3f4068304b4032bd428dd2cc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 566\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 566') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
